// 补充：获取历史年份对应年号的函数
function getEraName(year) {
    if (!year) return '';
    const y = parseInt(year);
    if (y === 184) return '中平元年';
    if (y === 189) return '中平六年';
    if (y === 190) return '初平元年';
    if (y === 191) return '初平二年';
    if (y === 192) return '初平三年';
    if (y === 194) return '兴平元年';
    if (y === 195) return '兴平二年';
    if (y === 196) return '建安元年';
    if (y === 197) return '建安二年';
    if (y === 198) return '建安三年';
    if (y === 199) return '建安四年';
    if (y === 200) return '建安五年';
    if (y === 202) return '建安七年';
    if (y === 207) return '建安十二年';
    if (y === 208) return '建安十三年';
    if (y === 210) return '建安十五年';
    if (y === 211) return '建安十六年';
    if (y === 214) return '建安十九年';
    if (y === 215) return '建安二十年';
    if (y === 219) return '建安二十四年';
    if (y === 221) return '章武元年';
    if (y === 222) return '章武二年';
    if (y === 223) return '建兴元年';
    if (y === 225) return '建兴三年';
    if (y === 227) return '建兴五年';
    if (y === 228) return '建兴六年';
    if (y === 229) return '建兴七年';
    if (y === 230) return '建兴八年';
    if (y === 231) return '建兴九年';
    if (y === 234) return '建兴十二年';
    if (y === 238) return '景初二年';
    if (y === 239) return '景初三年';
    if (y === 241) return '赤乌四年';
    if (y === 249) return '正始十年';
    if (y === 251) return '嘉平三年';
    if (y === 252) return '建兴元年';
    if (y === 253) return '建兴二年';
    if (y === 255) return '正元二年';
    if (y === 256) return '甘露元年';
    if (y === 257) return '甘露二年';
    if (y === 260) return '景元元年';
    if (y === 262) return '景元三年';
    if (y === 263) return '景元四年';
    if (y === 264) return '咸熙元年';
    if (y === 272) return '泰始八年';
    if (y === 279) return '咸宁五年';
    if (y === 280) return '太康元年';
    if (y === 290) return '太熙元年';
    return '未知年号';
}

const lowClasses = [
    '寻常教众', '黄巾力士', '普通士卒', '中军卒', '屯田客', '流民', '无籍流民', '白衣商贾',

    '河北步卒', '淮南步卒', '晋军士卒', '元从老卒', '寒门庶族', '军户', '白丁', '布衣', '平民', '屯田青壮',
    '随军老卒', '中军步卒', '蛮族雇佣兵', '死战之士', '江东水师'
];

function isLowClass(className) {
    if (!className) return false;
    for (let c of lowClasses) {
        if (className.includes(c)) return true;
    }
    return false;
}

    const assets = { name: '无', income: 0, expense: 0, food: 0, gold: 0 };
    if (!className) return assets;

    if (className.includes('割据军阀') || className.includes('割据首领') || className.includes('大贤良师') || className.includes('诸侯盟主') || className.includes('各路诸侯') || className.includes('坐山观虎斗之君') || className.includes('叛镇首领') || className.includes('霸府权臣') || className.includes('宗室权臣') || className.includes('大将军') || className.includes('大都督') || className.includes('东征主帅') || className.includes('北伐主帅')) {
        assets.name = '霸府金库与州郡税收'; assets.income = 50000; assets.expense = 40000; assets.food = 500000; assets.gold = 100000;

    else if (className.includes('司马氏宗王') || className.includes('汉室宗亲') || className.includes('州牧亲族') || className.includes('外镇都督') || className.includes('开国勋贵') || className.includes('平蜀大都督')) {

    }
    else if (className.includes('四世三公') || className.includes('江东世族') || className.includes('本土望族') || className.includes('辽东豪族') || className.includes('凉州豪族') || className.includes('外戚子弟')) {

function getClassOptionsByFaction(factionName) {
    const name = factionName || "";

    if (name.includes('残') || name.includes('余') || name.includes('亡国')) {
        if (name.includes('蜀') || name.includes('汉')) {
            return [{ name: '遗老孤臣', desc: '心怀故国，誓不降魏的旧臣' }, { name: '残兵败将', desc: '失了建制，流落山野的溃兵' }, { name: '死战之士', desc: '随姜维等将战至最后一刻的死士' }, { name: '隐世遗民', desc: '隐姓埋名，不问世事的百姓' }];
        }
        if (name.includes('三方') || name.includes('天下')) {
            return [{ name: '亡国旧臣', desc: '三国覆灭后苟活于世的降臣' }, { name: '山林隐士', desc: '看破红尘，隐居避世的高人' }, { name: '散兵游勇', desc: '天下虽定，依然落草为寇的乱兵' }];
        }
        return [{ name: '流亡部众', desc: '兵败后四处流窜的士卒' }, { name: '败军之将', desc: '丢城失地，仅带亲信逃亡的武将' }];
    }

    if (name.includes('援军') || name.includes('偷袭军')) {
        if (name.includes('东吴') || name.includes('孙') || name.includes('吴')) {
            return [{ name: '持节使臣', desc: '奉命出使联络的江东使节' }, { name: '江东水师', desc: '乘船溯江而上的水军精锐' }, { name: '解烦督将', desc: '统领精锐客军的东吴将校' }, { name: '白衣商贾', desc: '伪装成商人的水军精锐(偷袭专用)' }, { name: '客军部曲', desc: '远离故土作战的江东私兵' }];
        }
        if (name.includes('曹') || name.includes('魏')) {
            return [{ name: '驰援骁将', desc: '奉命日夜兼程赶赴前线的将领' }, { name: '中军精骑', desc: '曹魏中央军调拨的骑兵' }, { name: '运粮官', desc: '负责保障前线粮草的官员' }];
        }
        return [{ name: '客将', desc: '率军驰援他人的将领' }, { name: '客军士卒', desc: '随军远征的士兵' }];
    }

    if (name.includes('东征') || name.includes('伐吴') || name.includes('夷陵')) {
        if (name.includes('蜀') || name.includes('刘备')) {
            return [{ name: '东征主帅', desc: '统领大军顺江而下的最高统帅' }, { name: '复仇猛将', desc: '怀着满腔怒火冲锋陷阵的武将' }, { name: '随军老卒', desc: '随刘备征战半生的百战老兵' }, { name: '蛮族雇佣兵', desc: '被沙摩柯等统领的五溪蛮兵' }];
        }
        if (name.includes('吴') || name.includes('防御')) {
             return [{ name: '大都督', desc: '统筹全线防御的最高统帅' }, { name: '长江水营', desc: '依托长江天险防御的水军' }, { name: '解烦督将', desc: '统领精锐禁卫的将校' }];
        }
    }

    if (name.includes('南征') || name.includes('南蛮') || name.includes('孟获')) {
        if (name.includes('蜀') || name.includes('诸葛亮') || name.includes('汉')) {
            return [{ name: '南伐大将', desc: '统领南征大军的统帅' }, { name: '先锋悍将', desc: '逢山开路，遇水搭桥的猛将' }, { name: '随军参军', desc: '出谋划策的军中文职' }, { name: '远征士卒', desc: '水土不服的普通士兵' }];

            { name: '地方豪强', desc: '连阡阡陌，拥有大量田产与部曲的土豪' },
            { name: '宗族长者', desc: '主持宗族事务，德高望重的长辈' },
            { name: '世家子弟', desc: '凭借家族荫庇步入仕途的纨绔或俊杰' },
            { name: '坞堡堡主', desc: '结寨自保，统领乡里的实权人物' }
        ];
    }

    if (name.includes('派')) {
        if (name.includes('入蜀')) return [{ name: '荆州元从', desc: '随刘备入蜀的核心班底' }, { name: '先登猛将', desc: '冲锋陷阵的武将' }];
        if (name.includes('益州')) return [{ name: '本土士族', desc: '世代居住益州的豪强' }, { name: '东州兵', desc: '早年流入益州的客军' }];
        if (name.includes('挟天子')) return [{ name: '霸府权臣', desc: '掌控朝政的曹氏核心' }, { name: '汉室旧臣', desc: '名属汉臣实为曹臣的官员' }];
        if (name.includes('江东')) return [{ name: '淮泗旧将', desc: '孙策带来的江北将领' }, { name: '江东士族', desc: '江东本土门阀' }];
    }

    if (name.includes('汉朝廷') || name.includes('长安朝廷') || name.includes('许都朝廷') || name.includes('朝廷百官') || name.includes('保皇党') || name.includes('桓帝系') || name.includes('观望朝臣')) {
        return [{ name: '公卿大臣', desc: '位列三公九卿，掌握朝局动向' }, { name: '汉室宗亲', desc: '刘氏皇族血脉，身份尊贵' }, { name: '宿卫禁军', desc: '负责守卫皇宫的羽林军或虎贲军' }, { name: '清流名士', desc: '海内人望，不畏强权直言极谏' }, { name: '宦官党羽', desc: '依附十常侍等内廷势力的爪牙' }];
    }

    if (name.includes('曹魏政权') || name.includes('曹魏朝廷') || name.includes('司马氏')) {
        return [{ name: '公卿大臣', desc: '位列三公九卿的重臣' }, { name: '曹魏宗室', desc: '曹氏或夏侯氏核心' }, { name: '中军都督', desc: '统领洛阳中军的实权将领' }, { name: '世家子弟', desc: '九品中正制下得势的门阀子弟' }, { name: '宿卫禁军', desc: '驻守邺城或洛阳的禁军' }];
    }
    if (name.includes('东吴朝廷') || name.includes('东吴大军') || name.includes('孙氏')) {
        return [{ name: '江东世族', desc: '顾陆朱张等本土门阀领袖' }, { name: '公卿大臣', desc: '掌握江东朝政的重臣' }, { name: '水军都督', desc: '统领江东水师的核心统帅' }, { name: '解烦督将', desc: '统领精锐禁卫的将校' }];
    }
    if (name.includes('西晋朝廷') || name.includes('西晋初立')) {
        return [{ name: '司马氏宗王', desc: '司马家族的皇室核心' }, { name: '开国勋贵', desc: '助司马氏篡魏或平吴的功臣' }, { name: '外镇都督', desc: '镇守一方军政大权的封疆大吏' }, { name: '晋军士卒', desc: '晋朝常备军或水军' }];
    }
    if (name.includes('州郡') || name.includes('地方')) {
        return [
            { name: '本土望族', desc: '世代盘踞州郡，根基深厚的大族' },
            { name: '地方豪强', desc: '连阡阡陌，拥有大量田产与部曲的土豪' },
            { name: '州郡督将', desc: '掌管地方兵马的中层将官' },
            { name: '州牧亲族', desc: '割据长官的亲族子弟' },
            { name: '地方士人', desc: '在州郡内享有盛誉的饱学之士' }
        ];
    }

    if (name.includes('征') || name.includes('伐') || name.includes('灭')) {
        if (name.includes('蜀') || name.includes('诸葛') || name.includes('姜维') || name.includes('关羽')) {
            return [{ name: '北伐主帅', desc: '统领大军，克复中原的统帅' }, { name: '先锋悍将', desc: '逢山开路，遇水搭桥的猛将' }, { name: '运粮民夫', desc: '推着木牛流马艰难跋涉的役夫' }, { name: '无当飞军', desc: '擅长山地作战的南中精锐' }];
        }
        if (name.includes('曹魏') || name.includes('司马') || name.includes('西线')) {
            return [{ name: '平蜀大都督', desc: '手握重兵，统帅伐蜀大军的统帅' }, { name: '中军锐士', desc: '随司马氏出征的洛阳中军' }, { name: '关陇郡兵', desc: '被征发参战的雍凉兵马' }, { name: '随军参军', desc: '出谋划策的军中文职' }];
        }
        if (name.includes('西晋') && name.includes('灭吴')) {
            return [{ name: '楼船水师', desc: '王濬麾下顺江而下的水军' }, { name: '南伐大将', desc: '统率多路大军的晋军将帅' }, { name: '中军步卒', desc: '参与平吴战役的普通士兵' }];
        }
        return [{ name: '远征军主帅', desc: '统领全军的最高长官' }, { name: '先锋官', desc: '率领前锋部队的将领' }, { name: '远征士卒', desc: '离乡背井作战的普通士兵' }];
    }

    if (name.includes('守军') || name.includes('防御军')) {
        if (name.includes('合肥') || name.includes('樊城') || name.includes('曹') || name.includes('魏')) {
            return [{ name: '孤城守将', desc: '坚守重镇，死战不退的将领' }, { name: '敢死锐士', desc: '随张辽等将冲阵的敢死之士' }, { name: '屯田青壮', desc: '被临时征发上城墙的屯田客' }];
        }
        if (name.includes('吴') || name.includes('孙')) {
            return [{ name: '大都督', desc: '统筹全线防御的最高统帅' }, { name: '长江水营', desc: '依托长江天险防御的水军' }, { name: '江东部曲', desc: '将领自带的私家部曲' }];
        }
        return [{ name: '守城主将', desc: '负责城防的将领' }, { name: '守城士卒', desc: '驻守城池的士兵' }];
    }

    if (name.includes('宦官集团') || name.includes('宦官势力')) {
        return [{ name: '中常侍', desc: '权倾朝野的内廷首领' }, { name: '小黄门', desc: '宫中服侍、传达旨意的宦官' }, { name: '阉党亲信', desc: '依附宦官的地方官员或将领' }];
    }
    if (name.includes('外戚')) {
        return [{ name: '大将军', desc: '执掌天下兵马的外戚首领' }, { name: '外戚子弟', desc: '凭借家族势力占据要职' }, { name: '北军将士', desc: '听从外戚调遣的中央军' }];
    }

    if (name.includes('董卓') || name.includes('凉州军') || name.includes('李傕') || name.includes('郭汜')) {
        return [{ name: '凉州悍将', desc: '久经边塞战阵的西凉猛将' }, { name: '飞熊军士', desc: '董卓麾下最精锐的重骑兵' }, { name: '羌胡义从', desc: '归附西凉军阀的异族骑兵' }, { name: '朝廷降臣', desc: '迫于淫威投降董卓的汉室旧臣' }, { name: '西凉步卒', desc: '普通西凉籍贯的士卒' }];
    }

    if (name.includes('袁绍') || name.includes('冀州') || name.includes('关东诸侯')) {
        return [{ name: '四世三公', desc: '袁氏宗族或顶级门阀核心' }, { name: '冀州名士', desc: '河北大族的智谋之士' }, { name: '河北悍将', desc: '统领大戟士或先登的猛将' }, { name: '州郡督将', desc: '掌管地方兵马的中层将官' }, { name: '河北步卒', desc: '征发自冀、青、幽、并的士兵' }];
    }
    if (name.includes('袁术') || name.includes('宛城')) {
        return [{ name: '仲家伪臣', desc: '追随袁术称帝的伪朝官员' }, { name: '淮南上将', desc: '统领淮南大军的武将' }, { name: '淮南步卒', desc: '袁术麾下普通士兵' }];
    }

    if (name.includes('西晋') || name.includes('司马') || name.includes('晋')) {
        return [{ name: '司马氏宗王', desc: '司马家族的皇室核心' }, { name: '开国勋贵', desc: '助司马氏篡魏或平吴的功臣' }, { name: '中军都督', desc: '统领洛阳禁军的高级将领' }, { name: '外镇都督', desc: '镇守一方军政大权的封疆大吏' }, { name: '晋军士卒', desc: '晋朝常备军或水军' }];
    }

    if (name.includes('曹') || name.includes('魏') || name.includes('兖州')) {
        return [{ name: '宗族大将', desc: '曹氏或夏侯氏的核心统帅' }, { name: '颍川谋士', desc: '中原名门出身的顶级智囊' }, { name: '外姓悍将', desc: '五子良将等凭战功升迁的武将' }, { name: '虎豹骑', desc: '曹军最核心的精锐部队' }, { name: '青州兵', desc: '收编黄巾而来的悍勇之师' }, { name: '屯田客', desc: '受军屯编制的底层士兵' }];
    }

    if (name.includes('刘备') || name.includes('蜀') || name.includes('关羽') || name.includes('诸葛亮') || name.includes('姜维')) {
        return [{ name: '元从老卒', desc: '从涿县起兵就跟随刘备的嫡系' }, { name: '荆楚士人', desc: '刘备客居荆州时招揽的智囊' }, { name: '五虎上将', desc: '威震华夏的顶级武将' }, { name: '益州豪强', desc: '入蜀后收编的本土势力' }, { name: '白耳兵', desc: '蜀汉精锐部队' }];
    }

    if (name.includes('孙策') || name.includes('孙权') || name.includes('吴') || name.includes('江东')) {
        return [{ name: '江东世族', desc: '顾陆朱张等本土门阀领袖' }, { name: '淮泗旧将', desc: '孙坚孙策时期的江北元老' }, { name: '水军都督', desc: '统领江东水师的核心统帅' }, { name: '锦帆贼', desc: '甘宁统领的游侠水军' }, { name: '山越豪酋', desc: '盘踞山林被收编的越人首领' }];
    }

    if (name.includes('吕布')) {
        return [{ name: '并州狼骑', desc: '随吕布征战多年的并州骑兵' }, { name: '陷阵营', desc: '高顺统领的极锐重步兵' }, { name: '八健将', desc: '吕布麾下的核心武将' }, { name: '陈宫等谋士', desc: '辅佐吕布的智囊' }];
    }

    if (name.includes('公孙瓒')) {
        return [{ name: '白马义从', desc: '威震塞外的轻骑兵精锐' }, { name: '幽州突骑', desc: '常年抗击乌桓的边防骑兵' }, { name: '镇北守将', desc: '公孙瓒麾下武将' }];
    }
    if (name.includes('马超') || name.includes('马腾')) {
        return [{ name: '西凉铁骑', desc: '马家军的核心骑兵' }, { name: '羌族首领', desc: '敬服马超的羌人头领' }, { name: '凉州豪族', desc: '割据西北的地方势力' }];
    }
    if (name.includes('辽东')) {
        return [{ name: '公孙氏宗族', desc: '割据辽东的统治家族' }, { name: '辽东铁骑', desc: '常年与高句丽作战的骑兵' }];
    }

    if (name.includes('刘表') || name.includes('刘璋') || name.includes('张鲁') || name.includes('士燮') || name.includes('徐州') || name.includes('刘琮')) {
        return [{ name: '州牧亲族', desc: '割据长官的亲族子弟' }, { name: '本土望族', desc: '世代盘踞该州的名门' }, { name: '外来客将', desc: '依附州牧的中原将领' }, { name: '五斗米道', desc: '政教合一的信徒' }, { name: '地方水军', desc: '保境安民的州郡守军' }];
    }

    if (name.includes('在野') || name.includes('游侠') || name.includes('隐士')) {
        return [{ name: '隐世高人', desc: '隐居山林，洞悉天下的智者' }, { name: '绿林游侠', desc: '重然诺，轻生死，仗剑走天涯' }, { name: '避乱商贾', desc: '在乱世中贩运物资求生的商人' }, { name: '无籍流民', desc: '失去土地户籍，四处流浪' }];
    }

    return [{ name: '割据首领', desc: '该势力的最高统治者' }, { name: '军中猛将', desc: '冲锋陷阵的军事将领' }, { name: '幕府谋士', desc: '运筹帷幄的智囊团' }, { name: '精锐牙兵', desc: '主将的亲卫部队' }, { name: '普通士卒', desc: '大军中的寻常一兵' }];
}

 function getRegions(faction, mode, year, classLevel) {
    const fName = faction || "";
    if (classLevel) {
        if (classLevel.includes('残') || classLevel.includes('遗民') || classLevel.includes('旧臣') || classLevel.includes('败将') || classLevel.includes('流亡')) {
            return [
                {name: '深山老林', desc: '人迹罕至，躲避兵灾的绝佳之所'},
                {name: '偏僻坞堡', desc: '残存宗族自发结社自保的据点'},
                {name: '敌国都城', desc: '作为降将或俘虏被软禁监视之地'},
                {name: '乡野村落', desc: '隐姓埋名，苟延残喘的底层聚落'},
                {name: '边荒瘴地', desc: '逃避中原战火的极南或极北苦寒之地'}
            ];
        }
        if (classLevel.includes('隐士') || fName.includes('在野') || fName.includes('游侠')) {
            return [
                {name: '水镜庄', desc: '司马徽隐居，清谈纵论天下的名胜'},
                {name: '隆中', desc: '诸葛亮躬耕隐居之所'},
                {name: '繁华市井', desc: '大隐隐于市，冷眼旁观乱世的红尘闹市'},
                {name: '深山茅庐', desc: '采药炼丹，不问世事的化外仙境'},
                {name: '边塞荒漠', desc: '游侠儿纵马行侠的塞外风沙之地'},
                {name: '江湖草莽', desc: '藏污纳垢，三教九流汇聚的绿林地盘'}
            ];
        }
    }

    if (fName.includes('黄巾') || fName.includes('太平道')) {
        return [
            {name: '巨鹿', desc: '大贤良师张角传道大本营'},
            {name: '广宗', desc: '黄巾军主力与汉军决战的修罗场'},
            {name: '颖川', desc: '波才大破汉军的中原腹地'},
            {name: '汝南', desc: '黄巾肆虐的富庶大郡'},
            {name: '青州', desc: '百万青州黄巾流窜劫掠的齐鲁大地'}
        ];
    }
    if (fName.includes('南蛮') || fName.includes('孟获')) {
        return [
            {name: '建宁', desc: '南中四郡核心，雍闿叛乱之地'},
            {name: '云南', desc: '深入不毛，孟获大军盘踞的毒泉瘴地'},
            {name: '泸水', desc: '诸葛亮五月渡泸的险恶江河'}
        ];
    }

    if (year >= 189 && year <= 192) {
        if (fName.includes('董卓') || fName.includes('李傕') || fName.includes('凉州军')) {
            return [
                {name: '洛阳', desc: '被董卓付之一炬的东汉旧都'},
                {name: '长安', desc: '挟持献帝西迁后的新都'},
                {name: '郿坞', desc: '董卓囤积二十年粮食的坚固壁垒'},
                {name: '西凉', desc: '董卓军发迹的苦寒老巢'}
            ];
        }
        if (fName.includes('联军') || fName.includes('袁绍')) {
            return [
                {name: '酸枣', desc: '关东诸侯歃血为盟的大营'},
                {name: '渤海', desc: '袁绍起兵讨董的大本营'},
                {name: '虎牢关', desc: '联军与吕布血战的天下第一雄关'},
                {name: '汜水关', desc: '关羽温酒斩华雄的险关'}
            ];
        }
    }

    if (year >= 194 && year <= 199) {
        if (fName.includes('孙策') || fName.includes('刘繇') || fName.includes('吴') || fName.includes('豪强')) {
            return [
                {name: '曲阿', desc: '刘繇的大本营，被孙策攻破'},
                {name: '历阳', desc: '孙策渡江前的屯兵要地'},
                {name: '神亭岭', desc: '孙策与太史慈生死单挑的险峻山岭'},
                {name: '会稽', desc: '王朗固守的江南大郡'},
                {name: '吴郡', desc: '严白虎盘踞，后被孙策扫平的江东重镇'}
            ];
        }
        if (fName.includes('刘备') || fName.includes('吕布') || fName.includes('徐州')) {
            return [
                {name: '下邳', desc: '徐州首府，吕布殒命的白门楼所在'},
                {name: '小沛', desc: '刘备暂借的屯兵小城'},
                {name: '彭城', desc: '徐州咽喉要冲'}
            ];
        }
        if (fName.includes('袁术')) {
            return [
                {name: '寿春', desc: '袁术僭越称帝的仲家伪都'},
                {name: '宛城', desc: '袁术早年盘踞的南阳重镇'}
            ];
        }
    }

    if (year >= 200 && year <= 202) {
        if (fName.includes('曹') || fName.includes('袁绍')) {
            return [
                {name: '官渡大营', desc: '曹袁两军百万大军对峙的营垒'},
                {name: '乌巢', desc: '袁绍囤积重兵粮草的关键死穴'},
                {name: '许都', desc: '曹操后方空虚的献帝都城'},
                {name: '邺城', desc: '袁绍富庶的大后方'}
            ];
        }
    }

    if (year >= 207 && year <= 208) {
        if (fName.includes('刘备') || fName.includes('刘表')) {
            return [
                {name: '新野', desc: '刘备蛰伏抗曹的最前线'},
                {name: '樊城', desc: '与新野互为唇齿的江北要塞'},
                {name: '长坂坡', desc: '赵云七进七出救主的修罗场'},
                {name: '当阳桥', desc: '张飞喝退曹家百万兵的木桥'},
                {name: '江夏', desc: '刘琦镇守，刘备败退后的落脚点'},
                {name: '江陵', desc: '刘表囤积粮草军械的荆州重镇'}
            ];
        }
        if (fName.includes('孙权') || fName.includes('吴') || fName.includes('联军')) {
            return [
                {name: '柴桑', desc: '周瑜训练水师的东吴大营'},
                {name: '赤壁', desc: '孙刘联军火烧曹船的决战江面'},
                {name: '乌林', desc: '曹操大军屯扎，最终被烈火吞噬的旱寨'},
                {name: '夏口', desc: '孙刘会盟抗曹的咽喉要地'}
            ];
        }
        if (fName.includes('曹') || fName.includes('魏')) {
            return [
                {name: '襄阳', desc: '刘琮举州投降后曹军接管的重镇'},
                {name: '乌林', desc: '曹军铁索连舟的水军大营'},
                {name: '华容道', desc: '曹操败军泥泞难行的死亡沼泽'}
            ];
        }

            '坞堡堡主': ['四周被饿红眼的黄巾乱军重重包围，坞堡内的水井干涸，家丁们已开始窃窃私语准备献你首级求生。']

function getClassCrises(year, faction, className) {
    const mode = userData.mode;
    let crises = [];

    let classCrises = [];
    if (mode === '正史' && crisisData.classSpecific['正史']) {
        for (let key in crisisData.classSpecific['正史']) {
            if (className.includes(key)) {
                classCrises = classCrises.concat(crisisData.classSpecific['正史'][key]);
                break;
            }
        }
    }

    let factionCrises = [];
    const modeData = crisisData.specific[mode];
    if (modeData && modeData[year]) {
        for (let key in modeData[year]) {
            if (faction.includes(key) || key.includes(faction) ||
                (faction.includes('刘备') && key.includes('蜀')) ||
                (faction.includes('曹') && key.includes('魏')) ||
                (faction.includes('孙') && key.includes('吴'))) {
                factionCrises = factionCrises.concat(modeData[year][key]);
            }
        }
    }

    const isLow = isLowClass(className);
    if (!isLow) {
        factionCrises = factionCrises.filter(c =>
            !c.includes('卫士') && !c.includes('士卒') && !c.includes('兵') && !c.includes('小卒') && !c.includes('推着')
        );
    }

    crises = classCrises.concat(factionCrises);

    if (crises.length === 0) {
        if (mode === '正史') {
            if (className.includes('流民') || className.includes('平民') || className.includes('布衣') || className.includes('白丁') || className.includes('寒门')) {
                crises.push('村中大旱出现易子而食，督农官的催粮队正挨家搜刮最后一粒粟米。');
            }
            else if (className.includes('首领') || className.includes('主帅') || className.includes('盟主') || className.includes('都督') || className.includes('君') || className.includes('军阀')) {
                crises.push('两名核心统兵大将为夺兵权暗中互投毒，强敌大军正向边境集结。');
            }
            else if (className.includes('臣') || className.includes('名士') || className.includes('世族') || className.includes('大族') || className.includes('公卿') || className.includes('宗亲')) {
                crises.push('政敌伪造你们通敌谋反的信件，廷尉府的甲士已包围了你的府邸。');
            }
            else if (className.includes('宦官') || className.includes('外戚') || className.includes('常侍') || className.includes('黄门')) {
                crises.push('朝廷政变，清洗乱党的密诏下达，九门封锁你连出城逃命的机会都没有。');
            }
            else if (className.includes('卒') || className.includes('军') || className.includes('骑') || className.includes('将') || className.includes('兵')) {
                crises.push('营中爆发严重伤寒，你负责掩埋同袍，发现其中还有活人被扔进坑里。');
            }
            else {
                crises.push('你撞破上官收受敌国贿赂，他暗中扣留你的保命物资准备让你死在荒野。');
            }
        } else {
            crises.push('你面临群雄环伺，大军粮草即将告罄，内部人心思变。');
        }
    }

    crises = [...new Set(crises)].slice(0, 4);
    return crises.map(c => ({ name: c, desc: '' }));
}

// ==================== 状态数据 ====================
let userData = {
    route: '',
    mode: '',
    name: '',
    zi: '',
    age: '',
    situation: null,
    faction: '',
    customFactionName: '',
    position: '',
    classLevel: '',
    region: '',
    customRegion: '',
    force: { name: '', power: '', subordinates: '' },
    assets: { name: '', income: 0, expense: 0, food: 0, gold: 0 },
    attributes: {},
    selectedTraits: [],
    customTrait: '',
    reputation: '',
    crisis: '',
    joyEntertain: '',
    joyCategory: '',
    joyPlay: ''
};

let currentPage = '0';
const totalPages = 10;

function goToPage(n) {
    document.querySelectorAll('#app.sango-wrapper .page').forEach(p => p.classList.remove('active'));
    document.getElementById('page-' + n)?.classList.add('active');
    currentPage = String(n);
    updateStepIndicator();
}

function updateStepIndicator() {
    const ind = document.getElementById('step-indicator');
    if (!ind) return;
    ind.innerHTML = '';
    if (currentPage === '0') {
        ind.style.display = 'none';
        return;
    }
    ind.style.display = 'flex';

    let isJoy = typeof currentPage === 'string' && currentPage.includes('joy');
    let isLord = typeof currentPage === 'string' && currentPage.includes('lord');
    let currentIdx = 0;
    let total = isJoy ? 5 : totalPages - 1;

    if (isJoy) {
        if (currentPage === 'joy-1') currentIdx = 1;
        else if (currentPage === 'joy-2') currentIdx = 2;
        else if (currentPage === 'joy-3') currentIdx = 3;
        else if (currentPage === 'joy-4' || currentPage === 'joy-5') currentIdx = 4;
        else if (currentPage === 'joy-summary') currentIdx = 5;
    } else if (isLord) {
        if (currentPage === 'lord-1') currentIdx = 2;
        else if (currentPage === 'lord-2') currentIdx = 3;
    } else {
        currentIdx = parseInt(currentPage);
    }

    for (let i = 1; i <= total; i++) {
        const d = document.createElement('div');
        d.className = 'step-dot';
        if (i === currentIdx || (currentPage === '9' && i === total)) d.classList.add('active');
        if (i < currentIdx || (currentPage === '9' && i < total)) d.classList.add('done');
        ind.appendChild(d);
    }
}

function selectCard(el, group, isMultiSelect = false) {
    if (el.classList.contains('disabled')) return;
    if (isMultiSelect) {
        el.classList.toggle('selected');
    } else {
        document.querySelectorAll(`#${group} .card, #${group} .sub-card, #${group} .crisis-card`).forEach(c => c.classList.remove('selected'));
        el.classList.add('selected');
    }
}

function renderCards(containerId, data, group, onSelect, isMultiSelect = false, cardClass = 'card') {
    const container = document.getElementById(containerId);
    container.innerHTML = '';
    data.forEach(item => {
        const card = document.createElement('div');
        card.className = cardClass;
        card.innerHTML = `<div class="card-title">${item.title || item.name}</div><div class="card-desc">${item.desc || item.effects || ''}</div>`;
        if (item.disabled) card.classList.add('disabled');
        card.onclick = () => {
            if (card.classList.contains('disabled')) return;
            selectCard(card, containerId, isMultiSelect);
            onSelect(item);
        };
        container.appendChild(card);
    });
}

function setupOriginPage() {
    const routes = [
        { name: '自创人物', desc: '白手起家，在这乱世中书写你的传奇。' },
        { name: '演绎主公', desc: '化身汉末群雄，统领千军万马争霸天下。' },
        { name: '纵情欢乐', desc: '不问天下大势，只图今朝醉卧美人膝。' }
    ];
    renderCards('route-choice-cards', routes, 'route-choice-cards', item => {
        userData.route = item.name;

        if (item.name === '纵情欢乐') {
            userData.mode = '纵情欢乐';
            document.getElementById('mode-choice-cards').style.display = 'none';
            document.getElementById('origin-details-custom').style.display = 'flex';
        } else {
            document.getElementById('mode-choice-cards').style.display = 'grid';
            document.getElementById('origin-details-custom').style.display = item.name === '自创人物' ? 'flex' : 'none';

            const modes = [
                { name: '正史', desc: '依据《三国志》，摒弃神异与演义修饰。' },
                { name: '演义', desc: '基于《三国演义》，体验传奇与英雄浪漫。' }
            ];
            renderCards('mode-choice-cards', modes, 'mode-choice-cards', m => {
                userData.mode = m.name;
            });
        }
    });
}

function saveOrigin() {
    if (!userData.route) { alert('请选择游玩路线'); return; }

    // 严格限制模式的值
    if (userData.route !== '纵情欢乐' && userData.mode !== '正史' && userData.mode !== '演义') {
        alert('请选择正史或演义模式');
        return;
    }

    if (userData.route === '纵情欢乐') {
        userData.name = document.getElementById('input-name').value.trim();
        userData.zi = document.getElementById('input-zi').value.trim();
        userData.age = document.getElementById('input-age').value.trim();
        if (!userData.name) { alert('请输入姓名'); return; }
        setupJoyClassPage();
        goToPage('joy-1');
        return;
    }

    if (userData.route === '自创人物') {
        userData.name = document.getElementById('input-name').value.trim();
        userData.zi = document.getElementById('input-zi').value.trim();
        userData.age = document.getElementById('input-age').value.trim();
        if (!userData.name) { alert('请输入姓名'); return; }
        setupSituationPage();
        goToPage('2');
    } else if (userData.route === '演绎主公') {
        setupLordPage();
        goToPage('lord-1');
    }
}

// ----------------- 演绎主公专有逻辑 -----------------
function setupLordPage() {
    const container = document.getElementById('lord-cards');
    container.innerHTML = '';
    const lords = Object.keys(lordData).map(k => ({ name: k, desc: lordData[k].zi ? '字' + lordData[k].zi : '一代枭雄' }));
    renderCards('lord-cards', lords, 'lord-cards', item => {
        userData.name = item.name;
        userData.zi = lordData[item.name].zi;
    });
}

function saveLord() {
    if (!userData.name || !lordData[userData.name]) { alert('请选择你要扮演的主公'); return; }
    setupLordSituationPage();
    goToPage('lord-2');
}

function setupLordSituationPage() {
    const container = document.getElementById('lord-situation-cards');
    container.innerHTML = '';
    const validYears = lordData[userData.name].scripts[userData.mode] || [];

    // 修改为：将年份和标题拼接起来再去匹配
    const situations = scriptData[userData.mode].filter(s => validYears.includes(s.year + s.title));

    if(situations.length === 0) {
        container.innerHTML = `<p style="color:var(--text-muted); font-size:var(--fs-base); text-align:center; width:100%;">该主公在此模式下暂无活动剧本。</p>`;
    } else {
        situations.forEach(s => {
            const card = document.createElement('div');
            card.className = 'card';
            card.style.textAlign = 'left';
            card.innerHTML = `
                <div class="card-title" style="text-align:center;">${s.year} - ${s.title}</div>
                <div class="card-desc" style="text-align:center;">${s.desc}</div>
            `;
            card.onclick = () => {
                selectCard(card, 'lord-situation-cards');
                userData.situation = s;
            };
            container.appendChild(card);
        });
    }
}

function saveLordSituation() {
    if (!userData.situation) { alert('请选择时代剧本'); return; }

    const scriptName = userData.situation.year + userData.situation.title;
    const details = lordData[userData.name].getDetails(scriptName, userData.mode);

    if (!details || Object.keys(details).length === 0) {
        alert('抱歉，该剧本的详细数据丢失了，请重新选择~');
        return;
    }

        /* ===== faction / force 互斥处理 ===== */
    if (details.force) {
        /* 有 force 字段 = 此时该主公是一方之主 */
        userData.faction = '自立山头';
        userData.customFactionName = details.force;
        userData.force = {
            name: details.force,
            power: details.power || '',
            subordinates: details.subordinates || ''
        };
    } else if (details.faction) {
        /* 有 faction 字段 = 此时依附他人 */
        userData.faction = details.faction;
        userData.customFactionName = details.faction;
        userData.force = {
            name: '',
            power: details.power || '',
            subordinates: details.subordinates || ''
        };
    }

    /* ===== classLevel 从数据读取而非写死 ===== */
    userData.classLevel = details.classLevel || '未知';
    userData.position = details.position || '无';
    userData.region = '自定义地域';
    userData.customRegion = details.region || '未知';
    userData.age = details.age ? String(details.age) : '未定';

    /* ===== 只有子嗣填到下方家族信息框，其余留空 ===== */
    document.getElementById('input-family-info').value = details.children ? ('子嗣：' + details.children) : '子嗣：无';
    document.getElementById('input-relations').value = '';
    document.getElementById('input-faction-dynamic').value = '';
    document.getElementById('input-custom').value = '';

    userData.reputation = details.reputation || '里闾称善';
    userData.crisis = details.crisis || '暂无';
    userData.attributes = details.attributes || {};
    userData.selectedTraits = details.selectedTraits || [];

    if (details.assets) {
        userData.assets = {
            name: details.assets.name || '无',
            income: details.assets.income || 0,
            expense: details.assets.expense || 0,
            food: details.assets.food || 0,
            gold: details.assets.gold || 0
        };
    } else {
        userData.assets = getHistoryAssets(userData.classLevel);
    }

    displaySummary();
    goToPage('9');
}

function goBackFromSummary() {
    if (userData.route === '演绎主公') {
        goToPage('lord-2');
    } else {
        if (userData.customSubordinate) {
            goToPage('sub-detail');
        } else {
            goToPage('sub-choice');
        }
    }
}

function setupSituationPage() {
    const container = document.getElementById('situation-cards');
    const guide = document.getElementById('situation-guide');
    container.innerHTML = '';
    guide.innerHTML = `你选择了 <strong>${userData.mode}</strong> 路线。<br>天下大势，浩浩荡荡。请选择你要降临的时代节点。`;

    const situations = scriptData[userData.mode];
    situations.forEach(s => {
        const card = document.createElement('div');
        card.className = 'card';
        card.style.textAlign = 'left';
        card.innerHTML = `
            <div class="card-title" style="text-align:center;">${s.year} - ${s.title}</div>
            <div class="card-desc" style="text-align:center;">${s.desc}</div>
        `;
        card.onclick = () => {
            selectCard(card, 'situation-cards');
            userData.situation = s;
        };
        container.appendChild(card);
    });
}

function saveSituation() {
    if (!userData.situation) { alert('请选择时代大势节点'); return; }
    setupFactionPage();
    goToPage('3');
}

function setupFactionPage() {
    const container = document.getElementById('faction-cards');
    container.innerHTML = '';
    document.getElementById('custom-faction-container').style.display = 'none';

    let factionsList = userData.situation.factions || [];
    const factionsData = factionsList.map(f => ({ name: f, desc: '' }));

    factionsData.push({ name: '补充更多阵营', desc: '自行输入其他的天下势力' });
    factionsData.push({ name: '自立山头', desc: '不依附他人，自己建基立业' });

    renderCards('faction-cards', factionsData, 'faction-cards', item => {
        userData.faction = item.name;
        if (item.name === '补充更多阵营') {
            document.getElementById('custom-faction-container').style.display = 'flex';
        } else {
            document.getElementById('custom-faction-container').style.display = 'none';
        }
    });
}

function saveFaction() {
    if (!userData.faction) {
        alert('请选择所属阵营');
        return;
    }

    if (userData.faction === '补充更多阵营') {
        const customName = document.getElementById('input-custom-faction').value.trim();
        if (!customName) {
            alert('请输入自定义阵营名称');
            return;
        }
        userData.customFactionName = customName;
    } else {
        userData.customFactionName = userData.faction;
    }

    const romanceContainer = document.getElementById('romance-position-container');
    const historyContainer = document.getElementById('history-position-container');
    const indepContainer = document.getElementById('independent-force-container');
    const p4Title = document.getElementById('page-4-title');
    const p4Guide = document.getElementById('page-4-guide');

    document.getElementById('input-romance-position').value = '';
    document.getElementById('input-romance-class').value = '';
    document.getElementById('input-history-position').value = '';
    document.getElementById('input-custom-class').value = '';
    document.getElementById('force-name').value = '';
    document.getElementById('force-power').value = '';
    document.getElementById('force-subordinates').value = '';
    userData.classLevel = '';

    if (userData.faction === '自立山头') {
        romanceContainer.style.display = 'none';
        historyContainer.style.display = 'none';
        indepContainer.style.display = 'flex';
        p4Title.innerText = '执掌势力';
        p4Guide.innerText = '单枪匹马，抑或统帅部众？你的力量将如何组织？';
    } else {
        indepContainer.style.display = 'none';
        p4Title.innerText = '身份与阶级';
        p4Guide.innerText = '王侯将相，宁有种乎？请先确定你的出身门第，再定官职高低。';

        if (userData.mode === '演义') {
            romanceContainer.style.display = 'flex';
            historyContainer.style.display = 'none';
        } else {
            romanceContainer.style.display = 'none';
            historyContainer.style.display = 'flex';

            const dynamicClassOptions = getClassOptionsByFaction(userData.customFactionName);
            dynamicClassOptions.push({ name: '补充阶级', desc: '以上皆非，自行设定出身' });

            renderCards('class-cards', dynamicClassOptions, 'class-cards', item => {
                userData.classLevel = item.name;
                if (item.name === '补充阶级') {
                    document.getElementById('custom-class-container').style.display = 'flex';
                } else {
                    document.getElementById('custom-class-container').style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
        }
    }

    goToPage('4');
}

function saveClass() {
    if (userData.faction === '自立山头') {
        if (!userData.force) userData.force = {};
        userData.force.name = document.getElementById('force-name').value.trim();
        userData.force.power = document.getElementById('force-power').value.trim();
        userData.force.subordinates = document.getElementById('force-subordinates').value.trim();

        if (!userData.force.name) {
            alert('请填写势力名称');
            return;
        }
        userData.position = '主公';
        userData.classLevel = '割据军阀';
        userData.assets = getHistoryAssets('割据军阀');
    } else {
        if (userData.mode === '演义') {
            userData.position = document.getElementById('input-romance-position').value.trim();
            userData.classLevel = document.getElementById('input-romance-class').value.trim();

            if (!userData.position || !userData.classLevel) {
                alert('请填写职位与阶级');
                return;
            }

            userData.assets = {
                name: document.getElementById('input-romance-asset-name').value.trim() || '寻常营生',
                income: parseInt(document.getElementById('input-romance-asset-income').value) || 0,
                expense: parseInt(document.getElementById('input-romance-asset-expense').value) || 0,
                food: parseInt(document.getElementById('input-romance-asset-food').value) || 0,
                gold: parseInt(document.getElementById('input-romance-asset-gold').value) || 0
            };

        } else {
            userData.position = document.getElementById('input-history-position').value.trim();

            if (!userData.classLevel) {
                alert('请选择出身阶级');
                return;
            }

            if (userData.classLevel === '补充阶级') {
                const customClass = document.getElementById('input-custom-class').value.trim();
                if (!customClass) {
                    alert('请输入自定义阶级');
                    return;
                }
                userData.classLevel = customClass;
            }

            const customAssetName = document.getElementById('input-history-asset-name').value.trim();
            if (customAssetName) {
                userData.assets = {
                    name: customAssetName,
                    income: parseInt(document.getElementById('input-history-asset-income').value) || 0,
                    expense: parseInt(document.getElementById('input-history-asset-expense').value) || 0,
                    food: parseInt(document.getElementById('input-history-asset-food').value) || 0,
                    gold: parseInt(document.getElementById('input-history-asset-gold').value) || 0
                };
            } else {
                userData.assets = getHistoryAssets(userData.classLevel);
            }
        }
    }

    // 修复：确保 assets 结构完整，避免进入第9页时读取 undefined 报错
    if (!userData.assets) {
        userData.assets = { name: '无', income: 0, expense: 0, food: 0, gold: 0 };
    } else {
        userData.assets.name = userData.assets.name || '无';
        userData.assets.income = userData.assets.income || 0;
        userData.assets.expense = userData.assets.expense || 0;
        userData.assets.food = userData.assets.food || 0;
        userData.assets.gold = userData.assets.gold || 0;
    }

    setupRegionPage();
    goToPage('5');
}

function setupRegionPage() {
    const container = document.getElementById('region-cards');
    container.innerHTML = '';
    userData.region = '';
    document.getElementById('custom-region-container').style.display = 'none';
    document.getElementById('input-custom-region').value = '';

    const regions = getRegions(userData.customFactionName, userData.mode, userData.situation.year, userData.classLevel);

    regions.push({ name: '自定义地域', desc: '输入你想降临的具体城池或关隘' });

    renderCards('region-cards', regions, 'region-cards', item => {
        userData.region = item.name;
        if (item.name === '自定义地域') {
            document.getElementById('custom-region-container').style.display = 'flex';
        } else {
            document.getElementById('custom-region-container').style.display = 'none';
        }
    });

    const firstCard = container.querySelector('.card:not(.disabled)');
    if (firstCard) firstCard.click();
}

function saveRegion() {
    if (!userData.region) {
        alert('请选择所在地域');
        return;
    }
    if (userData.region === '自定义地域') {
        const customRegion = document.getElementById('input-custom-region').value.trim();
        if (!customRegion) {
            alert('请输入自定义地域名称');
            return;
        }
        userData.customRegion = customRegion;
    } else {
        userData.customRegion = userData.region;
    }

    setupAttributesPage();
    goToPage('6');
}

function setupAttributesPage() {
    const container = document.getElementById('attr-selection-area');
    container.innerHTML = '';
    userData.attributes = {};

    attributesList.forEach(attr => {
        userData.attributes[attr] = 0;

        const group = document.createElement('div');
        group.className = 'attr-slider-group';

        const header = document.createElement('div');
        header.className = 'attr-header';
        header.innerHTML = `<div class="attr-name">${attr}</div>`;

        const numberInput = document.createElement('input');
        numberInput.className = 'attr-number-input';
        numberInput.type = 'number';
        numberInput.min = '-100';
        numberInput.max = '100';
        numberInput.value = '0';
        header.appendChild(numberInput);

        const slider = document.createElement('input');
        slider.className = 'attr-slider';
        slider.type = 'range';
        slider.min = '-100';
        slider.max = '100';
        slider.value = '0';
        slider.step = '1';

        const updateUI = (val) => {
            let num = parseInt(val, 10);
            if (isNaN(num)) num = 0;
            if (num > 100) num = 100;
            if (num < -100) num = -100;

            slider.value = num;
            numberInput.value = num;
            userData.attributes[attr] = num;
        };

        slider.addEventListener('input', (e) => updateUI(e.target.value));
        numberInput.addEventListener('input', (e) => updateUI(e.target.value));
        numberInput.addEventListener('blur', (e) => {
            if(e.target.value === '') updateUI(0);
        });

        group.appendChild(header);
        group.appendChild(slider);
        container.appendChild(group);
    });

    refreshTraits();
}

function refreshTraits() {
    const shuffled = traitsData.sort(() => 0.5 - Math.random());
    const selectedOptions = shuffled.slice(0, 8);

    userData.selectedTraits = [];
    const handler = (item, list) => {
        const idx = list.findIndex(i => i.name === item.name);
        if (idx > -1) list.splice(idx, 1);
        else list.push(item);
    };

    renderCards('traits-cards', selectedOptions, 'traits-cards', item => handler(item, userData.selectedTraits), true, 'sub-card');
}

function saveAttributes() {
    userData.customTrait = document.getElementById('input-custom-trait').value.trim();
    setupReputationPage();
    goToPage('7');
}

function setupReputationPage() {
    const container = document.getElementById('reputation-cards');
    container.innerHTML = '';

    const isLow = isLowClass(userData.classLevel);

    reputationLevels.forEach((rep) => {
        const card = document.createElement('div');
        card.className = 'card';
        card.innerHTML = `<div class="card-title">${rep.name}</div><div class="card-desc">${rep.desc}</div>`;

        if (isLow && rep.type === '清' && rep.level >= 3) {
            card.classList.add('disabled');
        } else {
            card.onclick = () => {
                selectCard(card, 'reputation-cards');
                userData.reputation = rep.name;
            };
        }
        container.appendChild(card);
    });

    const firstCard = container.querySelector('.card:not(.disabled)');
    if (firstCard) firstCard.click();
}

function saveReputation() {
    if (!userData.reputation) {
        alert('请选择声誉');
        return;
    }
    setupCrisisPage();
    goToPage('8');
}

function setupCrisisPage() {
    const container = document.getElementById('crisis-cards');
    container.innerHTML = '';
    document.getElementById('custom-crisis-container').style.display = 'none';

    const crises = getClassCrises(userData.situation.year, userData.customFactionName, userData.classLevel);

    crises.push({ name: '自定义危机', desc: '自行设定你当前面临的困境或挑战，书写你独特的磨难' });

    renderCards('crisis-cards', crises, 'crisis-cards', item => {
        userData.crisis = item.name;
        if (item.name === '自定义危机') {
            document.getElementById('custom-crisis-container').style.display = 'flex';
        } else {
            document.getElementById('custom-crisis-container').style.display = 'none';
        }
    }, false, 'crisis-card');

    const firstCard = container.querySelector('.crisis-card:not(.disabled)');
    if (firstCard) firstCard.click();
}

function saveCrisis() {
    if (!userData.crisis) {
        alert('请选择当前危机');
        return;
    }

    if (userData.crisis === '自定义危机') {
        const customCrisis = document.getElementById('input-custom-crisis').value.trim();
        if (!customCrisis) {
            alert('请详细描述你面临的自定义危机');
            return;
        }
        userData.crisis = customCrisis;
    }

    // 只有自创人物路线才进入自定义部下选择
    if (userData.route === '自创人物') {
        document.querySelectorAll('#sub-choice-cards .card').forEach(c => c.classList.remove('selected'));
        const noCard = document.querySelectorAll('#sub-choice-cards .card')[1];
        if(noCard) noCard.classList.add('selected');
        document.getElementById('sub-choice-val').value = 'no';
        goToPage('sub-choice');
    } else {
        displaySummary();
        goToPage('9');
    }
}

function saveSubChoice() {
    const choice = document.getElementById('sub-choice-val').value;
    if (choice === 'yes') {
        setupSubDetailPage();
        goToPage('sub-detail');
    } else {
        userData.customSubordinate = null;
        displaySummary();
        goToPage('9');
    }
}

function setupSubDetailPage() {
    const container = document.getElementById('sub-attr-area');
    container.innerHTML = '';
    if (!userData.customSubordinate) {
        userData.customSubordinate = { name: '', age: '', customInfo: '', attributes: {} };
        attributesList.forEach(attr => userData.customSubordinate.attributes[attr] = 0);
    }

    document.getElementById('sub-name').value = userData.customSubordinate.name || '';
    document.getElementById('sub-age').value = userData.customSubordinate.age || '';

    // 自定义文本框的回填
    const customInfoEl = document.getElementById('sub-custom-info');
    if(customInfoEl) {
        customInfoEl.value = userData.customSubordinate.customInfo || '';
    }

    attributesList.forEach(attr => {
        const val = userData.customSubordinate.attributes[attr] || 0;
        const group = document.createElement('div');
        group.className = 'attr-slider-group';

        const header = document.createElement('div');
        header.className = 'attr-header';
        header.innerHTML = `<div class="attr-name">${attr}</div>`;

        const numberInput = document.createElement('input');
        numberInput.className = 'attr-number-input';
        numberInput.type = 'number';
        numberInput.min = '-100';
        numberInput.max = '100';
        numberInput.value = val;
        header.appendChild(numberInput);

        const slider = document.createElement('input');
        slider.className = 'attr-slider';
        slider.type = 'range';
        slider.min = '-100';
        slider.max = '100';
        slider.value = val;
        slider.step = '1';

        const updateUI = (newVal) => {
            let num = parseInt(newVal, 10);
            if (isNaN(num)) num = 0;
            if (num > 100) num = 100;
            if (num < -100) num = -100;

            slider.value = num;
            numberInput.value = num;
            userData.customSubordinate.attributes[attr] = num;
        };

        slider.addEventListener('input', (e) => updateUI(e.target.value));
        numberInput.addEventListener('input', (e) => updateUI(e.target.value));
        numberInput.addEventListener('blur', (e) => {
            if(e.target.value === '') updateUI(0);
        });

        group.appendChild(header);
        group.appendChild(slider);
        container.appendChild(group);
    });
}

function saveSubDetail() {
    const name = document.getElementById('sub-name').value.trim();
    if (!name) {
        alert('请输入部下姓名');
        return;
    }
    userData.customSubordinate.name = name;
    userData.customSubordinate.age = document.getElementById('sub-age').value.trim();

    // 保存部下的自定义设定
    const customInfoEl = document.getElementById('sub-custom-info');
    if(customInfoEl) {
        userData.customSubordinate.customInfo = customInfoEl.value.trim();
    }

    displaySummary();
    goToPage('9');
}

function displaySummary() {
    const summaryInfo = document.getElementById('summary-info');

    let html = `
        <div class="edit-icon" onclick="openEditModal('normal')" title="修改设定">✎ 修改</div>
        <strong>游玩路线:</strong> ${userData.route || '未知'}<br>
        <strong>真名:</strong> ${userData.name || '未知'} ${userData.zi ? `(${userData.zi})` : ''}<br>
        <strong>年龄:</strong> ${userData.age || '未定'}<br>
        <strong>剧本方向:</strong> ${userData.mode || '未知'}<br>
    `;

    if (userData.situation) {
        const era = getEraName(userData.situation.year);
        html += `<strong>时代节点:</strong> ${era} (${userData.situation.year || ''}年) - ${userData.situation.title || ''}<br>`;
    } else {
        html += `<strong>时代节点:</strong> 未知<br>`;
    }

    if (userData.faction === '自立山头') {
        html += `<strong>自立势力:</strong> ${userData.force.name || '未命名'}<br>`;
        if (userData.force.power) html += `<strong>兵力:</strong> ${userData.force.power}<br>`;
        if (userData.force.subordinates) html += `<strong>部下:</strong> ${userData.force.subordinates}<br>`;
    } else {
        html += `<strong>所属阵营:</strong> ${userData.customFactionName || '未知'}<br>`;
    }

    html += `
        <strong>出身阶级:</strong> ${userData.classLevel || '未知'}<br>
        <strong>所在地域:</strong> ${userData.customRegion || '未知'}<br>
        <strong>当前职位:</strong> ${userData.position || '无'}<br>
    `;

    const attrArr = [];
    if (userData.attributes) {
        for(const [key, val] of Object.entries(userData.attributes)) {
            if(val !== 0) attrArr.push(`${key}${val > 0 ? '+' : ''}${val}`);
        }
    }
    html += `<strong>基础属性:</strong> ${attrArr.length > 0 ? attrArr.join('，') : '平庸之辈'}<br>`;

    let traitsArr = [];
    if (userData.selectedTraits && Array.isArray(userData.selectedTraits)) {
        traitsArr = userData.selectedTraits.map(t => `${t.name || ''}(${t.effects || ''})`);
    }
    if(userData.customTrait) traitsArr.push(userData.customTrait);
    html += `<strong>特殊禀赋:</strong> ${traitsArr.length > 0 ? traitsArr.join('，') : '无'}<br>`;

    html += `<strong>当世声誉:</strong> ${userData.reputation || '未知'}<br>`;

    if (userData.assets) {
        html += `<strong>资产状况:</strong> 产业：${userData.assets.name || '无'}，收入：${userData.assets.income || 0}，支出：${userData.assets.expense || 0}，储备(石)：${userData.assets.food || 0}，储备(金)：${userData.assets.gold || 0}<br>`;
    } else {
        html += `<strong>资产状况:</strong> 未知<br>`;
    }

    html += `<strong>当前危机:</strong> ${userData.crisis || '暂无'}<br>`;

    if (userData.customSubordinate) {
        const sub = userData.customSubordinate;
        const subAttrArr = [];
        for(const [key, val] of Object.entries(sub.attributes)) {
            if(val !== 0) subAttrArr.push(`${key}${val > 0 ? '+' : ''}${val}`);
        }
        html += `<br><strong>心腹部下:</strong> ${sub.name} (年龄: ${sub.age || '未知'})<br>`;
        html += `<strong>部下属性:</strong> ${subAttrArr.length > 0 ? subAttrArr.join('，') : '平庸之辈'}<br>`;
        if (sub.customInfo) {
            html += `<strong>部下设定:</strong> ${sub.customInfo}<br>`;
        }
    }

    summaryInfo.innerHTML = html;
}

function formatUserDataAsContent() {
    let lines = [];
    const displayName = userData.name;
    lines.push('[用户角色信息]');

    if (userData.mode === '纵情欢乐') {
        lines.push(`剧本模式: 纵情欢乐`);
        lines.push(`姓名: ${displayName || '未定'}`);
        if(userData.zi) lines.push(`表字: ${userData.zi}`);
        if(userData.age) lines.push(`年龄: ${userData.age}`);
        lines.push(`出身阶级: ${userData.classLevel}`);
        lines.push(`所在地域: ${userData.region}`);
        lines.push(`娱乐方式: ${userData.joyEntertain}`);
        if(userData.joyCategory) lines.push(`声伎品类: ${userData.joyCategory}`);
        if(userData.joyPlay) lines.push(`专属玩法: ${userData.joyPlay}`);
        lines.push(`资产状况: 产业(${userData.assets.name}), 收入(${userData.assets.income}), 支出(${userData.assets.expense}), 储备石(${userData.assets.food}), 储备金(${userData.assets.gold})`);
    } else {
        lines.push(`游玩路线: ${userData.route}`);
        lines.push(`剧本模式: ${userData.mode}`);
        const era = getEraName(userData.situation.year);
        lines.push(`时代节点: ${era} (${userData.situation.year}年) - ${userData.situation.title}`);
        lines.push(`姓名: ${displayName || '未定'}`);
        if(userData.zi) lines.push(`表字: ${userData.zi}`);
        if(userData.age) lines.push(`年龄: ${userData.age}`);

        if (userData.faction === '自立山头') {
            lines.push(`势力归属: 自立 - ${userData.force.name || '未命名'} (兵力: ${userData.force.power || '无'})`);
            if(userData.force.subordinates) lines.push(`核心部下: ${userData.force.subordinates}`);
        } else {
            lines.push(`势力归属: 依附 - ${userData.customFactionName || '未知'}`);
        }

        lines.push(`出身阶级: ${userData.classLevel}`);
        lines.push(`所在地域: ${userData.customRegion}`);
        lines.push(`当前职位: ${userData.position || '无'}`);
        lines.push(`当世声誉: ${userData.reputation}`);

        const attrArr = [];
        for(const [key, val] of Object.entries(userData.attributes)) {
            if(val !== 0) attrArr.push(`${key}${val > 0 ? '+' : ''}${val}`);
        }
        lines.push(`基础属性: ${attrArr.length > 0 ? attrArr.join('，') : '平庸之辈'}`);

        const traitsArr = userData.selectedTraits.map(t => `${t.name}(${t.effects})`);
        if(userData.customTrait) traitsArr.push(userData.customTrait);
        lines.push(`特殊禀赋: ${traitsArr.length > 0 ? traitsArr.join('，') : '无'}`);

        lines.push(`资产状况: 产业(${userData.assets.name}), 收入(${userData.assets.income}), 支出(${userData.assets.expense}), 储备石(${userData.assets.food}), 储备金(${userData.assets.gold})`);
        lines.push(`当前危机: ${userData.crisis}`);

        if (userData.customSubordinate) {
            const sub = userData.customSubordinate;
            const subAttrArr = [];
            for(const [key, val] of Object.entries(sub.attributes)) {
                if(val !== 0) subAttrArr.push(`${key}${val > 0 ? '+' : ''}${val}`);
            }
            lines.push(`心腹部下: ${sub.name} (年龄: ${sub.age || '未知'})`);
            lines.push(`部下属性: ${subAttrArr.length > 0 ? subAttrArr.join('，') : '平庸之辈'}`);
            if (sub.customInfo) lines.push(`部下设定: ${sub.customInfo}`);
        }
    }

    if (userData.family_info) lines.push(`家族情况: ${userData.family_info}`);
    if (userData.relations) lines.push(`人际关系: ${userData.relations}`);
    if (userData.faction_dynamic) lines.push(`阵营动态: ${userData.faction_dynamic}`);
    if (userData.custom) lines.push(`其他设定: ${userData.custom}`);

    return lines.join('\n');
}

function formatUserDataAsMessage() {
    let lines = [];
    const displayName = userData.name;

    if (userData.mode === '纵情欢乐') {
        lines.push('我的纵情欢乐设定已完成，请根据以下设定开始推演：\n');
        lines.push('【基础身份】');
        lines.push(`我是 ${displayName}${userData.zi ? `（字${userData.zi}）` : ''}${userData.age ? `，年方${userData.age}岁` : ''}，出身${userData.classLevel}阶级。`);
        lines.push(`我身处风月无边的${userData.region}。`);
        lines.push('\n【资产状况】');
        lines.push(`我名下拥有产业：${userData.assets.name}。`);
        lines.push(`每月收入：${userData.assets.income}金，支出：${userData.assets.expense}金。`);
        lines.push(`目前储备粮草：${userData.assets.food}石，金银：${userData.assets.gold}金。`);
        lines.push('\n【极乐之境】');
        lines.push(`我选择的娱乐方式是：${userData.joyEntertain}。`);
        if(userData.joyCategory) lines.push(`偏好的声伎品类为：${userData.joyCategory}。`);
        if(userData.joyPlay) lines.push(`我专属的隐秘玩法是：${userData.joyPlay}。`);
        lines.push('\n请直接为我展现这声色犬马的极乐之境。');
    } else if (userData.route === '演绎主公') {
        lines.push('我的主公设定已就绪，请根据以下设定开始推演三国乱世：\n');
        lines.push('【基础身份】');
        lines.push(`剧本方向：${userData.mode}`);
        const era = getEraName(userData.situation.year);
        lines.push(`时间节点：${era} (${userData.situation.year}年) - ${userData.situation.title}`);

        if (userData.faction === '自立山头') {
            lines.push(`我是 ${displayName}${userData.zi ? `（字${userData.zi}）` : ''}，作为一方雄主身处${userData.customRegion}。`);
        } else {
            lines.push(`我是 ${displayName}${userData.zi ? `（字${userData.zi}）` : ''}，身处${userData.customFactionName}阵营的${userData.customRegion}。`);
        }

        lines.push(`出身为${userData.classLevel}，目前的身份地位是${userData.position}。`);
        lines.push(`我的当世声誉为“${userData.reputation}”。`);

        const attrArr = [];
        for(const [key, val] of Object.entries(userData.attributes)) {
            if(val !== 0) attrArr.push(`${key}${val > 0 ? '+' : ''}${val}`);
        }
        lines.push(`基础属性：${attrArr.length > 0 ? attrArr.join('，') : '平庸之辈'}`);

        const traitsArr = userData.selectedTraits.map(t => `${t.name}(${t.effects})`);
        if(userData.customTrait) traitsArr.push(userData.customTrait);
        lines.push(`特殊禀赋：${traitsArr.length > 0 ? traitsArr.join('，') : '无'}`);

        lines.push('\n【势力与资产】');
        if (userData.faction === '自立山头') {
            lines.push(`我自己建立了一方势力：${userData.force.name || '未命名'}。`);
            if(userData.force.power) lines.push(`手中握有兵力：${userData.force.power}。`);
            if(userData.force.subordinates) lines.push(`核心部下有：${userData.force.subordinates}。`);
        } else {
            lines.push(`我目前依附于：${userData.customFactionName || '未知'}。`);
        }

        lines.push(`产业名：${userData.assets.name}`);
        lines.push(`收入：${userData.assets.income}  支出：${userData.assets.expense}`);
        lines.push(`储备(石)：${userData.assets.food}  储备(金)：${userData.assets.gold}`);

        lines.push('\n【当前处境】');
        lines.push(`我目前面临的危机是：${userData.crisis}。`);
    } else {
        lines.push('我的角色信息已确定，请根据以下设定开始推演三国乱世：\n');
        lines.push('【基础身份】');
        lines.push(`剧本方向：${userData.mode}`);
        const era = getEraName(userData.situation.year);
        lines.push(`时间节点：${era} (${userData.situation.year}年) - ${userData.situation.title}`);
        lines.push(`我是 ${displayName}${userData.zi ? `（字${userData.zi}）` : ''}${userData.age ? `，年方${userData.age}岁` : ''}，身处${userData.customFactionName}阵营的${userData.customRegion}。`);
        lines.push(`出身为${userData.classLevel}，目前的身份地位是${userData.position || '布衣'}。`);
        lines.push(`我的当世声誉为“${userData.reputation}”。`);

        const attrArr = [];
        for(const [key, val] of Object.entries(userData.attributes)) {
            if(val !== 0) attrArr.push(`${key}${val > 0 ? '+' : ''}${val}`);
        }
        lines.push(`基础属性：${attrArr.length > 0 ? attrArr.join('，') : '平庸之辈'}`);

        const traitsArr = userData.selectedTraits.map(t => `${t.name}(${t.effects})`);
        if(userData.customTrait) traitsArr.push(userData.customTrait);
        lines.push(`特殊禀赋：${traitsArr.length > 0 ? traitsArr.join('，') : '无'}`);

        lines.push('\n【势力与资产】');
        if (userData.faction === '自立山头') {
            lines.push(`我自己建立了一方势力：${userData.force.name || '未命名'}。`);
            if(userData.force.power) lines.push(`手中握有兵力：${userData.force.power}。`);
            if(userData.force.subordinates) lines.push(`核心部下有：${userData.force.subordinates}。`);
        } else {
            lines.push(`我所属的阵营是：${userData.customFactionName || '未知'}。`);
        }

        lines.push(`产业名：${userData.assets.name}`);
        lines.push(`收入：${userData.assets.income}  支出：${userData.assets.expense}`);
        lines.push(`储备(石)：${userData.assets.food}  储备(金)：${userData.assets.gold}`);

        lines.push('\n【当前处境】');
        lines.push(`我目前面临的危机是：${userData.crisis}。`);

        if (userData.customSubordinate) {
            const sub = userData.customSubordinate;
            const subAttrArr = [];
            for(const [key, val] of Object.entries(sub.attributes)) {
                if(val !== 0) subAttrArr.push(`${key}${val > 0 ? '+' : ''}${val}`);
            }
            lines.push('\n【心腹部下】');
            lines.push(`我有一位誓死追随的部下，名为 ${sub.name}${sub.age ? `，年方${sub.age}岁` : ''}。`);
            lines.push(`其能力属性为：${subAttrArr.length > 0 ? subAttrArr.join('，') : '平庸之辈'}。`);
            if (sub.customInfo) lines.push(`关于此人的特殊设定：${sub.customInfo}`);
        }
    }

    if(userData.family_info || userData.relations || userData.faction_dynamic || userData.custom) {
        lines.push('\n【其他补充】');
        if(userData.family_info) lines.push(`家族情况：${userData.family_info}`);
        if(userData.relations) lines.push(`人际关系：${userData.relations}`);
        if(userData.faction_dynamic) lines.push(`阵营动态：${userData.faction_dynamic}`);
        if(userData.custom) lines.push(`特殊设定：${userData.custom}`);
    }

    if (userData.mode !== '纵情欢乐') {
        lines.push('\n乱世的齿轮已经转动，请描述我当下面临的具体情境与抉择。');
    }

    return lines.join('\n');
}

function onConfirm() {
    userData.family_info = document.getElementById('input-family-info').value.trim();
    userData.relations = document.getElementById('input-relations').value.trim();
    userData.faction_dynamic = document.getElementById('input-faction-dynamic').value.trim();
    userData.custom = document.getElementById('input-custom').value.trim();

    try {
        const charWB = getCharWorldbookNames('current');
        const wbName = charWB.primary;
        if (!wbName) {
            alert('当前角色卡未绑定主世界书，无法写入用户信息条目。\n请先为角色卡绑定一本世界书。');
            return;
        }
        deleteWorldbookEntries(wbName, (entry) => entry.name === '用户信息').then(() => {
            return createWorldbookEntries(wbName, [{
                name: '用户信息',
                enabled: true,
                strategy: { type: 'constant' },
                position: { type: 'before_character_definition' },
                content: formatUserDataAsContent(),
            }]);
        }).then(() => {
            return createChatMessages([{ role: 'user', message: formatUserDataAsMessage() }]);
        }).then(() => {
            return triggerSlash('/send');
        }).catch((err) => {
            alert('操作失败: ' + (err.message || String(err)));
            console.error('[角色创建] onConfirm error:', err);
        });
    } catch(e) {
        console.log('Final User Data:', formatUserDataAsMessage());
        alert('API调用失败，请确认在正确的环境中运行。\n' + e.message + '\n\n角色设定已输出至控制台。');
    }
}

// ==================== 纵情欢乐专属逻辑 ====================

function setupJoyClassPage() {
    userData.classLevel = '';
    userData.assets = { name: '', income: 0, expense: 0, food: 0, gold: 0 };
    renderCards('joy-class-cards', joyData.classes, 'joy-class-cards', item => {
        userData.classLevel = item.name;
        userData.assets = item.assets;
    });
}

function saveJoyClass() {
    if (!userData.classLevel) { alert('请选择阶级'); return; }
    setupJoyRegionPage();
    goToPage('joy-2');
}

function setupJoyRegionPage() {
    userData.region = '';
    renderCards('joy-region-cards', joyData.regions, 'joy-region-cards', item => {
        userData.region = item.name;
    });
}

function saveJoyRegion() {
    if (!userData.region) { alert('请选择地域'); return; }
    setupJoyEntertainPage();
    goToPage('joy-3');
}

function setupJoyEntertainPage() {
    userData.joyEntertain = '';
    userData.joyCategory = '';
    userData.joyPlay = '';
    renderCards('joy-entertain-cards', joyData.entertainments, 'joy-entertain-cards', item => {
        userData.joyEntertain = item.name;
        userData._isSex = item.isSex;
    });
}

function saveJoyEntertain() {
    if (!userData.joyEntertain) { alert('请选择娱乐方式'); return; }
    if (userData._isSex) {
        setupJoyCategoryPage();
        goToPage('joy-4');
    } else {
        displayJoySummary();
        goToPage('joy-summary');
    }
}

function setupJoyCategoryPage() {
    userData.joyCategory = '';
    const cats = joyData.categories[userData.joyEntertain] || [];
    renderCards('joy-category-cards', cats, 'joy-category-cards', item => {
        userData.joyCategory = item.name;
    });
}

function saveJoyCategory() {
    if (!userData.joyCategory) { alert('请选择声伎品类'); return; }
    setupJoyPlayPage();
    goToPage('joy-5');
}

function setupJoyPlayPage() {
    userData.joyPlay = '';
    const plays = joyData.plays[userData.joyCategory] || [];
    renderCards('joy-play-cards', plays, 'joy-play-cards', item => {
        userData.joyPlay = item.name;
    }, false, 'crisis-card');
}

function saveJoyPlay() {
    if (!userData.joyPlay) { alert('请选择专属玩法'); return; }
    displayJoySummary();
    goToPage('joy-summary');
}

function goBackFromJoySummary() {
    if (userData._isSex) {
        goToPage('joy-5');
    } else {
        goToPage('joy-3');
    }
}

function displayJoySummary() {
    const summaryInfo = document.getElementById('joy-summary-info');
    let html = `
        <div class="edit-icon" onclick="openEditModal('joy')" title="修改设定">✎ 修改</div>
        <strong>姓名:</strong> ${userData.name}<br>
        <strong>年龄:</strong> ${userData.age || '未知'}<br>
        <strong>表字:</strong> ${userData.zi || '无'}<br>
        <strong>产业:</strong> ${userData.assets.name}<br>
    `;
    if (userData.joyPlay) html += `<strong>玩法:</strong> ${userData.joyPlay}<br>`;
    if (userData.joyCategory) html += `<strong>品类:</strong> ${userData.joyCategory}<br>`;
    html += `
        <strong>方式:</strong> ${userData.joyEntertain}<br>
        <strong>阶级:</strong> ${userData.classLevel}<br>
        <strong>地域:</strong> ${userData.region}<br>
        <strong>收入:</strong> ${userData.assets.income} 金/月<br>
        <strong>支出:</strong> ${userData.assets.expense} 金/月<br>
        <strong>粮储:</strong> ${userData.assets.food} 石<br>
        <strong>金储:</strong> ${userData.assets.gold} 金<br>
    `;
    summaryInfo.innerHTML = html;
}

            alert('当前角色卡未绑定主世界书，无法写入用户信息条目。\n请先为角色卡绑定一本世界书。');
            return;
        }
        deleteWorldbookEntries(wbName, (entry) => entry.name === '用户信息').then(() => {
            return createWorldbookEntries(wbName, [{
                name: '用户信息',
                enabled: true,
                strategy: { type: 'constant' },
                position: { type: 'before_character_definition' },
                content: formatUserDataAsContent(),

}

function showPreviewModal() {
    userData.family_info = document.getElementById('input-family-info').value.trim();
    userData.relations = document.getElementById('input-relations').value.trim();
    userData.faction_dynamic = document.getElementById('input-faction-dynamic').value.trim();
    userData.custom = document.getElementById('input-custom').value.trim();

    const modal = document.getElementById('preview-modal');
    const textarea = document.getElementById('preview-textarea');
    const copyBtn = document.getElementById('btn-copy');

    textarea.value = formatUserDataAsMessage();

    copyBtn.innerText = '复制信息';
    copyBtn.style.borderColor = 'var(--theme-main)';
    copyBtn.style.color = 'var(--theme-main)';

    modal.classList.add('show');
}

function showJoyPreviewModal() {
    userData.family_info = document.getElementById('input-joy-family-info').value.trim();
    userData.relations = document.getElementById('input-joy-relations').value.trim();
    userData.faction_dynamic = document.getElementById('input-joy-faction-dynamic').value.trim();
    userData.custom = document.getElementById('input-joy-custom').value.trim();

    const modal = document.getElementById('preview-modal');
    const textarea = document.getElementById('preview-textarea');
    const copyBtn = document.getElementById('btn-copy');

    textarea.value = formatUserDataAsMessage();

    copyBtn.innerText = '复制信息';
    copyBtn.style.borderColor = 'var(--theme-main)';
    copyBtn.style.color = 'var(--theme-main)';

    modal.classList.add('show');
}

function closePreviewModal() {
    document.getElementById('preview-modal').classList.remove('show');
}

function copyPreviewText() {
    const textarea = document.getElementById('preview-textarea');
    const copyBtn = document.getElementById('btn-copy');

    textarea.select();
    textarea.setSelectionRange(0, 99999);

    try {
        navigator.clipboard.writeText(textarea.value).then(() => {
            copyBtn.innerText = '复制成功！';
            copyBtn.style.borderColor = 'var(--text-secondary)';
            copyBtn.style.color = 'var(--text-secondary)';
        }).catch(err => {
            document.execCommand('copy');
            copyBtn.innerText = '复制成功！';
        });
    } catch (err) {
        document.execCommand('copy');
        copyBtn.innerText = '复制成功！';
    }
}

// ==================== 编辑修改功能逻辑 ====================
let currentEditMode = 'normal';

function openEditModal(mode) {
    currentEditMode = mode;
    const container = document.getElementById('edit-form-container');
    container.innerHTML = '';

    let fields = [];
    if (mode === 'normal') {
        fields = [
            { key: 'name', label: '姓名', type: 'text' },
            { key: 'zi', label: '表字', type: 'text' },
            { key: 'age', label: '年龄', type: 'text' },
            { key: 'customFactionName', label: '所属阵营', type: 'text' },
            { key: 'classLevel', label: '出身阶级', type: 'text' },
            { key: 'customRegion', label: '所在地域', type: 'text' },
            { key: 'position', label: '当前职位', type: 'text' },
            { key: 'reputation', label: '当世声誉', type: 'text' },
            { key: 'crisis', label: '当前危机', type: 'textarea' },
            { key: 'asset_name', label: '产业名称', type: 'text', isAsset: true, assetKey: 'name' },
            { key: 'asset_income', label: '月收入(金)', type: 'number', isAsset: true, assetKey: 'income' },
            { key: 'asset_expense', label: '月支出(金)', type: 'number', isAsset: true, assetKey: 'expense' },
            { key: 'asset_food', label: '粮草储备(石)', type: 'number', isAsset: true, assetKey: 'food' },
            { key: 'asset_gold', label: '金银储备(金)', type: 'number', isAsset: true, assetKey: 'gold' }
        ];

        // 如果是自立山头或演绎主公，额外显示势力信息
        if (userData.faction === '自立山头') {
            fields.splice(7, 0,
                { key: 'force_name', label: '势力名称', type: 'text', isForce: true, forceKey: 'name' },
                { key: 'force_power', label: '兵力数量', type: 'text', isForce: true, forceKey: 'power' },
                { key: 'force_sub', label: '核心部下', type: 'text', isForce: true, forceKey: 'subordinates' }
            );
        }

        // 动态添加属性输入框
        attributesList.forEach(attr => {
            fields.push({ key: 'attr_' + attr, label: '属性: ' + attr, type: 'number', isAttr: true, attrKey: attr });
        });

        // 如果有自定义部下，也加入编辑列表
        if (userData.customSubordinate) {
            fields.push({ key: 'sub_name', label: '部下姓名', type: 'text', isSub: true, subKey: 'name' });
            fields.push({ key: 'sub_age', label: '部下年龄', type: 'text', isSub: true, subKey: 'age' });
            attributesList.forEach(attr => {
                fields.push({ key: 'sub_attr_' + attr, label: '部下属性: ' + attr, type: 'number', isSubAttr: true, attrKey: attr });
            });
            fields.push({ key: 'sub_customInfo', label: '部下设定', type: 'textarea', isSub: true, subKey: 'customInfo' });
        }

    } else {
        // 纵情欢乐模式字段
        fields = [
            { key: 'name', label: '姓名', type: 'text' },
            { key: 'zi', label: '表字', type: 'text' },
            { key: 'age', label: '年龄', type: 'text' },
            { key: 'classLevel', label: '阶级', type: 'text' },
            { key: 'region', label: '地域', type: 'text' },
            { key: 'joyEntertain', label: '娱乐方式', type: 'text' },
            { key: 'joyCategory', label: '声伎品类', type: 'text' },
            { key: 'joyPlay', label: '专属玩法', type: 'text' },
            { key: 'asset_name', label: '产业名称', type: 'text', isAsset: true, assetKey: 'name' },
            { key: 'asset_income', label: '月收入(金)', type: 'number', isAsset: true, assetKey: 'income' },
            { key: 'asset_expense', label: '月支出(金)', type: 'number', isAsset: true, assetKey: 'expense' },
            { key: 'asset_food', label: '粮草储备(石)', type: 'number', isAsset: true, assetKey: 'food' },
            { key: 'asset_gold', label: '金银储备(金)', type: 'number', isAsset: true, assetKey: 'gold' }
        ];
    }

    // 遍历生成输入框
    fields.forEach(f => {
        let val = '';
        if (f.isAsset) {
            val = userData.assets[f.assetKey] !== undefined ? userData.assets[f.assetKey] : '';
        } else if (f.isForce) {
            val = userData.force[f.forceKey] || '';
        } else if (f.isAttr) {
            val = userData.attributes[f.attrKey] !== undefined ? userData.attributes[f.attrKey] : 0;
        } else if (f.isSub) {
            val = userData.customSubordinate[f.subKey] || '';
        } else if (f.isSubAttr) {
            val = userData.customSubordinate.attributes[f.attrKey] !== undefined ? userData.customSubordinate.attributes[f.attrKey] : 0;
        } else {
            val = userData[f.key] || '';
        }

        let inputHtml = '';
        if (f.type === 'textarea') {
            inputHtml = `<textarea id="edit-input-${f.key}" class="edit-form-input" style="min-height: 80px; resize: vertical;">${val}</textarea>`;
        } else {
            inputHtml = `<input type="${f.type}" id="edit-input-${f.key}" class="edit-form-input" value="${val}">`;
        }

        container.innerHTML += `
            <div class="edit-form-group">
                <label class="edit-form-label">${f.label}</label>
                ${inputHtml}
            </div>
        `;
    });

    document.getElementById('edit-modal').classList.add('show');
}

function closeEditModal() {
    document.getElementById('edit-modal').classList.remove('show');
}

function saveEditedInfo() {
    // 重新收集表单数据
    const inputs = document.getElementById('edit-form-container').querySelectorAll('.edit-form-input');
    inputs.forEach(el => {
        const id = el.id.replace('edit-input-', '');
        let val = el.value.trim();

        if (el.type === 'number') {
            val = parseInt(val) || 0;
        }

        if (id.startsWith('asset_')) {
            const key = id.replace('asset_', '');
            userData.assets[key] = val;
        } else if (id.startsWith('force_')) {
            const key = id.replace('force_', '');
            userData.force[key] = val;
        } else if (id.startsWith('attr_')) {
            const key = id.replace('attr_', '');
            userData.attributes[key] = val;
        } else if (id.startsWith('sub_attr_')) {
            const key = id.replace('sub_attr_', '');
            userData.customSubordinate.attributes[key] = val;
        } else if (id.startsWith('sub_')) {
            const key = id.replace('sub_', '');
            userData.customSubordinate[key] = val;
        } else {
            userData[id] = val;
        }
    });

    closeEditModal();

    // 根据模式刷新界面
    if (currentEditMode === 'normal') {
        displaySummary();
    } else {
        displayJoySummary();
    }
}

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    document.getElementById('start-button').addEventListener('click', () => goToPage('1'));
    setupOriginPage();
    updateStepIndicator();
});
</script>
</body>
</html>
